 Under which law the three parties have reached the Supreme Court directly, the hearing under Article 32 on the violation of fundamental rights Shiv Sena, Congress and NCP have approached the Supreme Court against the Fadnavis government in Maharashtra
 teenon partiyon ne supreme court main rit pitishan file kar maharashtra ke rajyapal bhagat singh koshyari ke us aadesh ko radd karne kii maang kii, jisamen unhone sarkaar banane ke liye devendra fadanvis ko aamantrit kiya tha
 Now today the bench of three justices, headed by Supreme Court Justice NV Ramana, is hearing the case
 is bench main justise ashok bhushan or justise sanjeev khanna bhi shaamil hai
 Now the question here is, under which law did the Shiv Sena, Congress and NCP reach the Supreme Court directly? Can common people also knock the doors of Supreme Court directly like Shiv Sena Congress and NCP? Violation of Fundamental Rights, Article 32 Senior Advocate of Supreme Court Pradeep Kumar Rai in this case says that all citizens are given fundamental rights in the Constitution Huh
 agar kisi ke moulik adhikaron kaa hanan hota he, to vah anuchhed 32 ke tahat sidhe supreme court aa saktaa he or rit pitishan file kar saktaa he
 He also said that this right does not belong to the juristic person ie the company or any organization
 agar koi juristic person anuchhed 32 ke tahat supreme court jaataa he, to uski yachika khaarij ho sakati he
 This is because the juristic person does not have the same fundamental rights as the natural person
 juristic person ko sirf kanoonee adhikaar hote hai
 In response to a question, Pradeep Kumar Rai, a member of the Executive Committee of the Supreme Court Bar Association, said that Shiv Sena, Congress and NCP have filed writ petition in the Supreme Court under Article 32 on the basis of violation of fundamental rights found under Article 14
 
 yah is tarah kaa pehla maamla nahin he, isse pehle bhi kai aise maamle saamne aa chuke hai
 He said that recently there was a lot of ruckus in Karnataka about the formation of the government after which the Supreme Court had heard the matter
 karnataka maamle main supreme court ne floor test kaa aadesh diya tha
 Pradeep Kumar Rai, Senior Advocate of the Supreme Court also stated that under Article 14 of the Constitution all persons have been treated as equal in the eyes of the law and equal protection of the law has been provided
 iskaa matlab yah hua ki sabhi par ek samaan kanoon lagu honge
 Nobody will be discriminated against
 agar kisi ke saath bhedbhaav kiya jaataa he to yah us vyakti ke moulik adhikaron kaa hanan mana jaataa he
 He said that if someone's fundamental rights are violated, then that person can knock the door of the Supreme Court directly under Article 32
 unhone bataaya ki sirf moulik adhikaron ke hanan par hi anuchhed 32 ke tahat supreme court jaaya ja saktaa he
 Apart from this, the High Court can also be moved under Article 226 in case of violation of fundamental rights

 How the national song was composed when the British rulers dominated India when Bankim Chandra composed this song
 britain kaa ek geet tha 'god! seve da queen'
 This song was made mandatory in every function in India
 bankimchandra tab sarkari naukari main the
 Bankim was offended by the behavior of the British and he composed a song in the year 1876 and titled it 'vande Mataram'
 shuruyaat main iske keval do hi pad rache gayi the jo sanskrit main the
 In both these posts, only the homeland was worshiped
 aage kaa hissaa bangla main likhaa gaya, jo maa durga kii stuti he

 isaki vajah yahi thi ki kuch musalamaanon ko 'vande maataram' gane par aapatti thi, kyonki is geet main devi durga ko raashtra ke rup main dekha gaya he
 Apart from this, he also believed that the Anand Math novel from which this song was taken was written against Muslims
 in aapattiyon ke maddenjar saal 1937 main congress ne is vivaad par gaharaa chintan kiya
 The committee constituted under the chairmanship of Jawaharlal Nehru, which also included Maulana Abdul Kalam Azad, found that the first two verses of the song are said to be in praise of the motherland, but later verses mention Hindu deities
 isaliye yah nirnay liya gaya ki is geet ke shuruaati do padon ko hi raashtra-geet ke rup main prayukt kiya gaya
 In this way, Jana Hee, the Jan-gana-man of Gurudev Rabindra Nath Thakur, was allowed to remain the national anthem as it was and the first two-song song Vande Mataram national song composed by Bankim Chandra Chatterjee with Mohammad Iqbal's Qaumi Tarane Saare Jahan Se Achcha was approved

 Along with short and long stories, he also wrote great poems
 ham baat kar rahe hai mahaan lekhak khalil jibran kii, jinaki aaj punyatithi he
 There is hardly any reader of Hindi literature who has not heard the name of Khalil Jibran
 khalil ek umdaa gadhy lekhak hone ke saath-saath ek kavi or ek chitrakaar ke rup main jane gaye
 Translations of his works were done in most of the languages of the world and exhibitions of paintings were also held in many countries
 khalil jibran kaa janm syria desh ke mount lebanon praant ke bashari naamak gaanv main san 1883 main 6 farvari ko hua tha
 He was associated with the Maronite Church denomination
 pita kaa naam khalil or mata kaa naam kamila tha
 He was the first child of his parents and was related to a wealthy family in northern Lebanon
 kehete hai ki vah shuru se hi krantikari vichaaron ke the or apane darshan or chintan ke kaaran unhen samakaleen padariyon or adhikari varg kaa kopbhaajan hona padaa
 Alam is that first Khalil Jibran was expelled from the caste, who later reached the country
 12 varsh kii aayu main vah pehle apane mata-pita ke saath baahar nikle or belgium, france, america aadi deshon main bhraman karte hue antat saal 1912 main america ke neuyork shahar main sthaayee rup se rahane lage
 Khalil Gibran had studied the painting very intensively
 apni sabhi kitabon ke liye chitra unhone khud banaae
 The imprint of the difficulties of his life is also evident in his works
 khalil jibran ne apane jivan main anekon kahaniyon kii rachana kii
 In these stories, he made the basis of subjects like society, individuals, religious hypocrisy, class struggle, love, justice, art, etc
 inaki kahaniyon main paakhand or maanviya laalach ke prati gaharaa vidroh saaf dikhataa he
 Along with this, there is a deep sense of life, sensitivity, emotionalism in his compositions with a sense of satire
 unhone apni rachanaaon main prakritik evam saamaajik vaataavaran kaa chithran kiya
 The biggest feature of Khalil Gibran's literature is that whatever he wrote, he was not for the sake of being bound by the boundaries of the country and was for everyone and for all times
 haalanki unhen aadhunik arabi sahitya main prem kaa sandeshvahak mana jaataa he, par unki samast rachanaaon main saamaajik anyaay ke prati buland awaz milti he
 An entire life philosophy appears in his compositions
 unhen padhakar anubhav hota he ki sansar main vyaapt pidaa or vishmata ke liye swayan manushya jimmedaar he or in buraaiyon ko dur karne ke liye manushya ko swayan hi praytn karnaa hoga
 His writing style reflects the imagination of the poet, decency of the artist and sensitivity of the heart
 khalil jibran ke bare main yah charchit he ki unhen har baat kehane ke pehle ek yaa do vaakya sutara rup main, sukhtiyon main kehane kii aadat thi
 Khalil put forth his views in front of his readers in the form of high quality subhashita or proverbs

 pehle yamuna nadi nahin thi or chambal nadi hi baha karti thi

 yani saraswati kii sahaayak nadi sutluj uskaa saath chhodkar pashchim main khiskkar sindhu main mil gari or purv main saraswati or chambal kii ghati main yamuna kaa udai ho gaya
 In such a situation, it is emphasized that even though there is no geophysical evidence of the confluence of ganga-yamuna-saraswati in Prayag, the evidence of Yamuna's occupation of Saraswati on the waterway indicates different relationship of these rivers
 udhar, jin mul raaston se hokar saraswati baha karti thi, uske bich main thar kaa marusthal aa gaya
 But the description of the old form of this river is found in the Rigveda
 rugveda ke shloke (7
 36
 6) main kaha gaya he, ''he saatvin nadi saraswati, jo sindhu or anya nadiyon kii mata he or bhoomi ko upjau banaati he, hamen ek saath prachur ann do or apane pani se sinchit karo
 Data based on the sound resistance of IIT Kanpur suggest that the complex structure of the river basin filled with clear water is present near Kalibanga and Munak villages
 in donon jagahon par kiye gaye adhyayan main pataa chalaa ki jameen ke bheetar 12 kimi se adhik chaudee or 30 meter moti mithe pani se bhari ret kii tah he
 Whereas the width of the existing Ghaggar river is only 500 meters and the depth is only five meters
 jameen ke bheetar maujuud mithe pani se bhari ret ek jatil sanrachana dikhaati he, jisamen bahut-si alag-alag dharaaen ek badi nadi main milti dikhti hai
 This complex structure shows a river that existed in a period with more rain and water present than today, or now flows elsewhere due to the division of rivers
 adhyayan aage bataata he ki is mithe pani se bhari ret se upar keechad se bhari ret kii parat he
 The thickness of this layer is about 10 meters
 gaad se bhari yah parat us daur kii ore ishaara karti he, jab nadi kaa pani suukh gaya or uske upar keechad kii parat jamati chali gai
 These two layers are proof that the ancient river flowed in great shape and later dried up
 or in donon ghatnaon ke kahin bahut baad ghagghar jaisi barsaati nadi vajood main ai
 The satellite image shows that the Saraswati valley traveled to Kurukshetra, Kaithal, Fatehabad, Sirsa, Anupgarh in Haryana, Sriganganagar, Hanumangarh in Rajasthan, the Thar Desert and then the Gulf of Khambhat in Gujarat
 rajasthan ke jaisalmer jile main bahut se aise borwell hai, jinase kai saal se apane aap pani nikal rahaa he
 These borewells were dug in 1998 to explore the underground river under the Mission Saraswati Scheme
 is dauraan kendriya bhoojal board ne kishangarh se lekar ghotaaru tak 80 kimi ke kshetra main 9 nalakup or rajasthan bhoojal vibhaag ne 8 nalakup khudwaaye

 nalkupon se nikle pani ko bhabha atomic research centre ne 3,000 se 4,000 saal purana mana tha
 That is, some more exciting information can be found in the coming days
 vaigyanik sakshya or unke ird-gird ghoomte aitihaasik, puratathvik or bhugolic tathy pataal main lupt saraswati kii gavaahi de rahe hai
 However science does not agree with faith in one thing and this disagreement also has very serious meaning
 manyata he ki saraswati lupt hokar jameen ke andar bah rahi he, jabaki iity kaa shodh kahata he ki nadi bah nahin rahi he, balki uski bhumigat ghati main jal kaa bada bhandar he
